           XX* Or a list of FILE() or PARMLIB() and colon : separated paths                
           XX*   in the form of                                                            
           XX*                                                                             
           XX*    +------------ : ------------+                                            
           XX*    V                           |                                            
           XX* >--+--FILE(ussPath)------------+--><                                        
           XX*    |                           |                                            
           XX*    +--PARMLIB(dsname(member))--+                                            
           XX*                                                                             
           XX* Example:                                                                    
           XX*   CONFIG=FILE(/my/long/path/to/1.yaml)\                                     
           XX*   :PARMLIB(ZOWE.PARMLIB(YAML))                                              
           XX*                                                                             
           XX* In the above case, the \ is used as a line continuation.                    
           XX*                                                                             
           XX* When using a list, files on left override properties                        
           XX* from files to their right.                                                  
           XX* Typically the right-most file should be the Zowe default yaml.
